/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_PersonelBelgeYonetimi]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_PersonelBelgeYonetimi](
@BelgeGrpIlkkod  nvarchar(25),
@BelgeGrpSonkod  nvarchar(25),
@BelgeGrpKodyapi nvarchar(25),
@PersIlkkod  nvarchar(25),
@PersSonkod  nvarchar(25),
@PersKodyapi nvarchar(25),
@BelgeIlkkod  nvarchar(25),
@BelgeSonkod  nvarchar(25),
@BelgeKodyapi nvarchar(25),
@Tarih  DateTime,
@Pozisyon tinyint = 0,    -- {0:Hepsi }
@Persnull_fl bit = 0,
@Persfull_fl bit = 0
)
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
bdt_Guid                                 AS [#msg_S_0088]   /* KAYIT NO */  ,
per_kod                                   AS [msg_S_0501\G] /* PERSONEL KODU */,
RTRIM(per_adi) + ' ' + RTRIM(per_soyadi)  AS [msg_S_0502]   /* PERSONEL ADI */ ,
per_dept_kod                              AS [#msg_S_0871]  /* DEPARTMAN KODU */,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_cikis_tar) AS [#msg_S_0758] /* ÇIKIS TAR. */ ,
(Select pdp_adi from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod) AS [#msg_S_0872] /* DEPARTMAN ADI*/ ,
per_bolge_kodu AS [#msg_S_1036] /* BÖLGE KODU */ ,
(select pbl_bolge_adi from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu) AS [#msg_S_1177] /* BÖLGE ADI*/ ,
per_kim_gorev AS [#msg_S_1700] /* GÖREV KODU */ ,
(select pgk_gorev_adi from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev) AS [#msg_S_0898] /* GÖREV ADI*/,
bel_kod                             AS [msg_S_2741]   /* BELGE KODU */,
bel_isim                                  AS [msg_S_2742]   /* BELGE İSMİ */,
Case When ((bdt_Guid is not null) and (bdt_Guid <> cast(0x0 as uniqueidentifier))) Then dbo.fn_GetResource('P',2308,DEFAULT) ELSE dbo.fn_GetResource('R',0266,DEFAULT) end As [msg_S_4361] /*BELGE DURUMU*/,
bdt_belge_no                              AS [msg_S_0093]   /* BELGE NO */,
bdt_belge_yeri                            AS [msg_S_2743]   /* BELGE VERİLİŞ YERİ */,
bdt_ulke_kodu                             AS [msg_S_0905]   /* ÜLKE KODU */,
CASE WHEN dbo.fn_ValidDate(bdt_belge_baslangic) = 1
THEN bdt_belge_baslangic
ELSE @Tarih
END                                       AS [msg_S_0307]   /* VERİLİŞ TARİHİ */,
CASE WHEN dbo.fn_ValidDate(bdt_belge_bitis) = 1
THEN bdt_belge_bitis
ELSE @Tarih
END                                       AS [msg_S_0265]   /* BİTİŞ TARİHİ */,
CASE WHEN dbo.fn_ValidDate(bdt_belge_bitis) = 1
THEN dbo.fn_gunfarkibul(@Tarih,bdt_belge_bitis)
ELSE NULL
END                                       AS [msg_S_2744]   /* KALAN GÜN*/ ,
dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('E',4152,bdt_pozisyon+1,DEFAULT)  AS [msg_S_2745]   /* BELGE POZİSYONU */ ,
bdt_sorumlu                               AS [msg_S_2746]   /* SORUMLU PERSONEL KODU  */ ,
CASE WHEN bdt_sorumlu<>'' THEN dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,bdt_sorumlu)
ELSE ''
END                                       AS [#msg_S_2747] /* SORUMLU PERSONEL İSMİ */,
CASE WHEN dbo.fn_ValidDate(bdt_pozisyon_degisim_tarihi) = 1
THEN bdt_pozisyon_degisim_tarihi
ELSE NULL
END                                       AS [msg_S_2748]   /* POZİSYON DEĞİŞİM TARİHİ */ ,
bdt_pozisyon_aciklama                     AS [msg_S_2749]   /* POZİSYON AÇIKLAMASI */ ,
bgr_kod                                   AS [msg_S_0135]  /* GRUP KODU*/,
bgr_isim                                  AS [msg_S_0136]  /* GRUP adı*/,
Data                                      AS [msg_S_1252]/* RESİM*/
FROM  dbo.PERSONELLER CROSS JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_BELGE_TANIMLARI  WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_BELGE_GRUPLARI ON bgr_belge_kod=bel_kod
LEFT OUTER HASH JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_BELGE_DETAYLARI  ON (per_kod = bdt_pers_kod and bdt_belge_kod=bel_kod )
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.mye_ImageData ON (TableID=bdt_fileid AND Record_uid=bdt_Guid)
WHERE ( (@Persnull_fl=0)  OR ((@Persnull_fl=1) and (bdt_pers_kod is NOT NULL)) ) AND
( (@Pozisyon=0)or(@Pozisyon=bdt_pozisyon+1)) AND
( ( (bgr_kod >= @BelgeGrpIlkkod) or (@BelgeGrpIlkkod='') ) and
( (bgr_kod <= @BelgeGrpSonkod) or (@BelgeGrpSonkod='') ) and
( (bgr_kod LIKE dbo.fn_KodYapidanWhere(@BelgeGrpKodyapi)) or (@BelgeGrpKodyapi='') ) )  AND
( ( (bdt_pers_kod >= @PersIlkkod) or (@PersIlkkod='') ) and
( (bdt_pers_kod <= @PersSonkod) or (@PersSonkod='') ) and
( (bdt_pers_kod LIKE dbo.fn_KodYapidanWhere(@PersKodyapi)) or (@PersKodyapi='') ) ) AND
( ( (bdt_belge_kod >= @BelgeIlkkod) or (@BelgeIlkkod='') ) and
( (bdt_belge_kod <= @BelgeSonkod) or (@BelgeSonkod='') ) and
( (bdt_belge_kod LIKE dbo.fn_KodYapidanWhere(@BelgeKodyapi)) or (@BelgeKodyapi='') ) ) AND
( (@Persfull_fl=0) or (@Persfull_fl=1 and dbo.fn_ValidDate(per_cikis_tar)=0))
)
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI_CHOOSE_3]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_PerTahakkukKupu]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_PerTahakkukKupu](@PersKesin as bit)
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT
TOP 100 PERCENT
pt_pkod AS [msg_S_0501] /* PERSONEL KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,pt_pkod) AS [msg_S_0502] /* PERSONEL ADI */ ,
dbo.fn_SSK_Adi(per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [msg_S_0621] /* SSK ŞUBESİ */ ,
dbo.fn_PerIsGrubu(per_is_grup) AS [msg_S_0622] /* İŞ GRUBU */ ,
IsNull(per_dept_kod  + (select case when pdp_adi is not null Then ' / '+pdp_adi End
from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod),'') AS [msg_S_0513] /* DEPARTMAN */ ,
IsNull(per_bolge_kodu + (select case when pbl_bolge_adi is not null Then ' / '+pbl_bolge_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI WITH (NOLOCK) where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu),'') AS [msg_S_0514] /* BÖLGE */ ,
IsNull(per_kim_gorev + (select case when pgk_gorev_adi is not null Then ' / '+pgk_gorev_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev),'') AS [msg_S_0515] /* GÖREV */ ,
per_muh_kod AS [msg_S_1027] /* MUH. KODU */ ,
per_kim_meslek AS [msg_S_0761] /* MESLEK */ ,
Per_TcKimlikNo AS [#msg_S_0766] /* T.C.KİMLİK NO */ ,
Per_PersMailAddress AS [#msg_S_0767] /* E-POSTA ADR. */ ,
CASE WHEN per_Brut_net = 0
THEN RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,1,DEFAULT)) /* Brütten nete */
ELSE RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,2,DEFAULT)) /* Netten brüte */
END AS [#msg_S_0769] /* ÜCRET TİPİ */ ,
CASE WHEN per_ucr_bode_yapilma = 0
THEN RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',472,1,DEFAULT)) /* Yapılmasın */
ELSE RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',472,2,DEFAULT)) /* Yapılsın */
END AS [#msg_S_0770] /* BANK.ÖDEME */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',221, DEFAULT), per_tip+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_0077] /* TİPİ */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',466, DEFAULT), per_kim_tahsil+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1590]/* TAHSİLİ*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',470, DEFAULT), per_kim_sakat_derece+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1592] /*SAKATLIK DERECESİ*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',474, DEFAULT), per_kim_gocmen+1, DEFAULT)       AS [#msg_S_1593] /*GÖÇMEN KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',468, DEFAULT), per_kim_gorev_kod+1, DEFAULT)    AS [#msg_S_0897] /*GÖREV KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',469, DEFAULT), per_kim_SGK_kod+1, DEFAULT)      AS [#msg_S_1594] /*SGK KODU*/,
per_ucr_send_durum            AS [#msg_S_1605] /*SENDİKA DURUMU*/,
per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr          AS [#msg_S_1607] /*SİGORTA % GRUBU*/,
per_ucr_vdaire                AS [#msg_S_0881] /*VERGİ DAİRESİ */,
per_ucr_konutfon              AS [#msg_S_1380] /*KONUT FONU        */,
per_ucr_onceod                AS [#msg_S_1610] /*ÖNCE ÖDM. KF. AYI             */,
per_yard_yol                  AS [#msg_S_1611] /*YOL YARIDMI           */,
per_yard_yemek                AS [#msg_S_1612] /*YEMEK YARDIMI         */,
per_yard_yakacak              AS [#msg_S_1613] /*YAKACAK YARDIMI          */,
per_yard_bayram               AS [#msg_S_1614] /*BAYRAM YARDIMI*/,
per_yard_cocuk                AS [#msg_S_1615] /*COCUK YARIDIMI*/,
per_yard_aile                 AS [#msg_S_1616] /*AİLE YARDIMI*/,
per_yard_ozelindirim          AS [#msg_S_1617] /*ÖZEL İNDRİM*/,
per_doviz_cinsi               AS [#msg_S_0849] /*DÖVİZ CİNSİ*/,
per_VkfKesOd_fl               AS [#msg_S_1620] /*VAKIF KESİNTİSİ UYGULANDI	*/,
per_iszlksig                  AS [#msg_S_1622] /*İŞSİZLİK SİGORTASI        */,
per_Calismatipi               AS [#msg_S_1623] /*ÇALIŞMA TİPİ              */,
per_mevsim                    AS [#msg_S_1624] /*ÇALIŞMA DÖNEMİ            */,
per_tabiioldugukanun          AS [#msg_S_1629] /*TABİİ OLDUĞU KANUN        */,
per_IdariAmirKodu             AS [#msg_S_1626] /*İDARİ AMİR KODU           */,
per_TeknikAmirKodu            AS [#msg_S_1627] /*TEKNİK AMİR KODU          */,
pt_maliyil             AS [msg_S_0517] /* MALİ YIL */ ,
dbo.fn_AyIsimBul(pt_tah_ay) AS [msg_S_0223] /* AY */ ,
CAST(pt_tahno  AS nvarchar) AS [msg_S_0623] /* PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI NO */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1602, DEFAULT), per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_1963]/*BAĞLI SRM MERKEZİ */ ,
CASE  per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip
WHEN 1 THEN per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu+' '+dbo.fn_SorumlulukMerkeziIsmi(per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu)
WHEN 2 THEN per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu+' '+(Select top 1 dan_ismi FROM dbo.DAGITIM_ANAHTARI_TANIMLARI  WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu=dan_kod)
ELSE null
END AS [msg_S_1962] /*SRM.MRK Veya DAĞ.ANAH*/,
SUM(pt_normalkazanc)   AS [msg_S_0624] /* KAZANÇ */ ,
SUM(pt_ekkazanc)       AS [msg_S_0625] /* EK KAZANÇ */ ,
SUM(pt_sosyrdm)        AS [msg_S_0626] /* SOSYAL YARDIM */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc)         AS [msg_S_0627] /* TOPLAM KAZANÇ */ ,
SUM(pt_verind)         AS [msg_S_0628] /* ÖZEL İNDİRİM */ ,
SUM(pt_sakverind)      AS [msg_S_0629] /* SAKATLIK İND. */ ,
SUM(pt_gocverind)      AS [msg_S_0630] /* GÖÇMEN İND. */ ,
SUM(pt_digverindgv+pt_hayatsigortasi+pt_digverinddv) AS [msg_S_0631] /* GV+HS+DV MUAFI */ ,
SUM(pt_digverindssk)   AS [msg_S_0632] /* SSK MUAFI */ ,
SUM(pt_toplamind)      AS [msg_S_0633] /* TOPLAM İNDİRİM */ ,
SUM(pt_sskprimi)       AS [msg_S_0634] /* SSK PRİMİ */ ,
SUM(pt_gv)             AS [msg_S_0635] /* GELİR VERGİSİ */ ,
SUM(pt_dv)             AS [msg_S_0636] /* DAMGA VERGİSİ */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt)         AS [msg_S_0637] /* ÖZEL KESİNTİ */ ,
SUM(pt_iszlksigperpayi)AS [msg_S_0640] /* İŞS.SİG.PER.PAYI */ ,
SUM(pt_iszlksigisvpayi)AS [msg_S_0641] /* İŞS.SİG.İŞV.PAYI */ ,
SUM(pt_digersigorta_isveren)   AS [msg_S_0642] /* DİĞER SİG.İND.İŞV */ ,
SUM(pt_digersigorta_calisan)   AS [msg_S_0665] /* DİĞER SİG.İND.ÇLŞ */ ,
SUM(pt_kesinti)        AS [msg_S_0643] /* TOPLAM KESİNTİ */ ,
SUM(pt_tersbakiye)     AS [msg_S_0644] /* TERS BAKİYE */ ,
SUM(pt_yuvfarki)       AS [msg_S_0645] /* YUVARLAMA FARKI */ ,
SUM(pt_asgarigecimindirimi)AS [msg_S_3148] /* AGİ */ ,
SUM(pt_net)            AS [msg_S_0646] /* NET */ ,
CAST(SUM(pt_sskgunu) AS float) AS [msg_S_0647] /* SSK GÜN */ ,
SUM(pt_sskbrutmatrah)  AS [msg_S_0648] /* SSK MATRAHI */ ,
SUM(pt_devsskmatrah)   AS [msg_S_0649] /* DEV.SSK.MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_gvbrut)         AS [msg_S_0650] /* GV MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_gvmatrah)       AS [msg_S_0651] /* TOPLAM GV MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_devgvmatrah)    AS [msg_S_0652] /* DEV.GV.MATRAH */ ,
CAST(SUM(pt_izingunu) AS float) AS [msg_S_0653] /* İZİN GÜNÜ */ ,
SUM(pt_izinmatrah)     AS [msg_S_0654] /* SSK İZİN MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_sskisvhis)      AS [msg_S_0655] /* SSK İŞV.HİSSESİ */ ,
SUM(pt_sskkonfon)      AS [msg_S_0656] /* SSK KONUT FONU */ ,
SUM(pt_bireyselsigorta_isveren)AS [msg_S_0657] /* BİREYSEL SİG.İND.İŞV */,
SUM(pt_bireyselsigorta_calisan)AS [msg_S_1470], /* BİREYSEL SİG.İND.ÇLŞ */
SUM(pt_ilave_agi)      AS [msg_S_4418] /* İLAVE EDİLEN AGİ */
FROM dbo.PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK) ON ( per_kod = pt_pkod )
WHERE ((pt_kesin = 1) or (@PersKesin = 1))
/*PAR3*/ --Dikkat bu aciklama kod icinden degistiriliyor kaldirmayin
GROUP BY pt_maliyil,pt_tah_ay,pt_pkod,per_ucr_PSSK_sube,per_is_grup,pt_tahno,per_dept_kod,per_bolge_kodu,per_kim_gorev,
per_muh_kod,per_kim_meslek ,Per_TcKimlikNo,Per_PersMailAddress,per_Brut_net,per_ucr_bode_yapilma,per_tip,per_kim_tahsil,
per_kim_gocmen,per_kim_gorev_kod,per_kim_SGK_kod,per_ucr_send_durum,per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr,per_ucr_vdaire,
per_ucr_konutfon,per_ucr_onceod,per_yard_yol,per_yard_yemek,per_yard_yakacak,per_yard_bayram,
per_yard_cocuk,per_yard_aile,per_yard_ozelindirim,per_doviz_cinsi,per_VkfKesOd_fl,per_iszlksig,
per_Calismatipi,per_mevsim,per_tabiioldugukanun,per_IdariAmirKodu,per_TeknikAmirKodu,per_kim_sakat_derece,
per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip,per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu
ORDER BY  pt_maliyil,pt_tah_ay,pt_pkod,per_ucr_PSSK_sube,per_is_grup,pt_tahno,per_dept_kod,per_bolge_kodu,per_kim_gorev,
per_muh_kod,per_kim_meslek ,Per_TcKimlikNo,Per_PersMailAddress,per_Brut_net,per_ucr_bode_yapilma,per_tip,per_kim_tahsil,
per_kim_gocmen,per_kim_gorev_kod,per_kim_SGK_kod,per_ucr_send_durum,per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr,per_ucr_vdaire,
per_ucr_konutfon,per_ucr_onceod,per_yard_yol,per_yard_yemek,per_yard_yakacak,per_yard_bayram,
per_yard_cocuk,per_yard_aile,per_yard_ozelindirim,per_doviz_cinsi,per_VkfKesOd_fl,per_iszlksig,
per_Calismatipi,per_mevsim,per_tabiioldugukanun,per_IdariAmirKodu,per_TeknikAmirKodu,per_kim_sakat_derece,
per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip,per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu
)
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSONELDILEKCE_YONETIMI]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/

CREATE VIEW [dbo].[PERSONELDILEKCE_YONETIMI]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
per_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
per_kod AS [msg_S_0078] /* KODU */ ,
per_adi AS [msg_S_0502] /* PERSONEL ADI */ ,
per_soyadi AS [msg_S_1064] /* PERSONEL SOYADI */ ,
per_orjdildeadisoyadi AS [msg_S_4766],
per_sicil_no       AS [msg_S_0755] /* SSK SİCİL NO */ ,
dbo.fn_SSK_Adi(per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [msg_S_0621] /* SSK ŞUBESİ */ ,
per_dept_kod AS [msg_S_0756] /* DEP.KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PerIsGrubu(per_is_grup) AS [msg_S_0622] /* İŞ GRUBU */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_giris_tar) AS [msg_S_0757] /* GİRİŞ TAR. */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_cikis_tar) AS [msg_S_0758] /* ÇIKIŞ TAR. */ ,
per_cikis_neden AS [msg_S_0759] /* ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ */ ,
per_muh_kod AS [msg_S_0760] /* MUH.KODU */ ,
per_kim_meslek AS [msg_S_0761] /* MESLEK */ ,
per_cikis_neden AS  [#msg_S_0759] /* ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',767, DEFAULT), per_CikisSebebiSecimli+1, DEFAULT)    AS [#msg_S_1641] /*ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ(SEÇİMLİ)*/,
per_muh_kod AS [msg_S_1027] /* MUH. KODU */ ,
IsNull(per_dept_kod  + (select case when pdp_adi is not null Then ' / '+pdp_adi End
from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod),'') AS [msg_S_0513] /* DEPARTMAN */ ,
IsNull(per_bolge_kodu + (select case when pbl_bolge_adi is not null Then ' / '+pbl_bolge_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI WITH (NOLOCK) where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu),'') AS [msg_S_0514] /* BÖLGE */ ,
IsNull(per_kim_gorev + (select case when pgk_gorev_adi is not null Then ' / '+pgk_gorev_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev),'') AS [msg_S_0515] /* GÖREV */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_nuf_dogum_tarih) AS [msg_S_0762] /* DOĞ.TAR. */ ,
per_nuf_dogum_yer AS [msg_S_0763] /* DOĞ.YERİ */ ,
per_ozel_not AS [msg_S_0451] /* ÖZEL NOT */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_Kidem_Tarih) AS [msg_S_0764] /* KIDEM TAR. */ ,
per_asgari_ucretli AS [msg_S_0765] /* ASGARİ ÜCT. */ ,
Per_TcKimlikNo AS [msg_S_0766] /* T.C.KİMLİK NO */ ,
Per_PersMailAddress AS [msg_S_0767] /* E-POSTA ADR. */ ,
Per_Muh_Grup_Kodu AS [msg_S_0768] /* MUHTASAR GRUP KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PersAktifCalismaKodu (per_kod) AS [msg_S_2504] /* AKTİF ÇALIŞMA KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',449,DEFAULT), per_Brut_net+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_2023] /*NET/BRÜT*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',472,DEFAULT), per_ucr_bode_yapilma+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_0770] /* BANK.ÖDEME */ ,
per_ucr_hesapno AS [msg_S_0771] /* HESAP NO */ ,
(select ssk_maasbankakodu from dbo.PERSONEL_SSK_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where ssk_Sira_No = per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [msg_S_0772] /* SSK BANKALAR */ ,
SGKBTipIsim AS [msg_S_4458], /*TABİ OLDUĞU SGK BELGE TÜRÜ*/
SGKKanunNoVeIsim AS [msg_S_4459], /*TABİ OLDUĞU SGK KANUNU*/
MKTipIsim AS [msg_S_4460],/*TABİ OLDUĞU MALİYE KANUNU*/
per_special1 AS [msg_S_0773] /* ÖZEL ALAN 1 */ ,
per_special2 AS [msg_S_0774] /* ÖZEL ALAN 2 */ ,
per_special3 AS [msg_S_0775] /* ÖZEL ALAN 3 */,
per_uye_dernek           AS [msg_S_1650] /*ÜYE OLDUĞU ODA/DERNEK*/,
per_uye_dernek_sicil_no   AS [msg_S_1651] /*ÜYE ODA/DERNEK SİCİL NO*/,
per_firma_no    AS [msg_S_1263] /* FİRMA NO */,
per_sube_no   AS [msg_S_1126] /* ŞUBE NO */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',221, DEFAULT), per_tip+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_0077] /* TİPİ */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',466, DEFAULT), per_kim_tahsil+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_1590]/* TAHSİLİ*/,
per_dil1 AS [msg_S_1642] /*TÜRKÇE    */,
per_dil2 AS [msg_S_1643] /*İNGİLİZCE */,
per_dil3 AS [msg_S_1644] /*ALMANCA   */,
per_dil4 AS [msg_S_1645] /*FRANSIZCA */,
per_dil5 AS [msg_S_1646] /*İTALYANCA */,
per_dil6 AS [msg_S_1647] /*İSPANYOLCA*/,
per_dil7 AS [msg_S_1648] /*RUSÇA     */,
per_dil8 AS [msg_S_1649] /*ARAPÇA    */,
per_dil9 AS [msg_S_2508] /*AZERİCE    */,
per_dil10 AS [msg_S_2509] /*GÜRCÜCE    */,
per_dil11 AS [msg_S_1500] /*DİĞER      */,
per_dil12 AS [msg_S_2510] /*DİĞER 2    */,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',470, DEFAULT), per_kim_sakat_derece+1, DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_1592] /*SAKATLIK DERECESİ*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',474, DEFAULT), per_kim_gocmen+1, DEFAULT)       AS [msg_S_1593] /*GÖÇMEN KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',468, DEFAULT), per_kim_gorev_kod+1, DEFAULT)    AS [msg_S_0897] /*GÖREV KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',469, DEFAULT), per_kim_SGK_kod+1, DEFAULT)      AS [msg_S_1594] /*SGK KODU*/,
per_kim_cocuk                 AS [msg_S_1595] /*ÇOCUK ADEDİ*/,
per_kim_okuloncesi            AS [msg_S_1596] /*ÇOCUK AD(OKUL ÖNCESİ)*/,
per_kim_ilkokul               AS [msg_S_1597] /*ÇOCUK AD(İLKÖĞRETİM)*/,

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSDETAY_gizli]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[PERSDETAY_gizli]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
per_kod AS [msg_S_0078] /* KODU */ ,
per_adi + ' ' + per_soyadi AS [msg_S_0070] /* İSMİ */ ,
per_sicil_no       AS [#msg_S_0755] /* SSK SİCİL NO */ ,
dbo.fn_SSK_Adi(per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [#msg_S_0621] /* SSK ŞUBESİ */ ,
per_dept_kod AS [#msg_S_0756] /* DEP.KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PerIsGrubu(per_is_grup) AS [#msg_S_0622] /* İŞ GRUBU */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_giris_tar) AS [#msg_S_0757] /* GİRİŞ TAR. */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_cikis_tar) AS [#msg_S_0758] /* ÇIKIŞ TAR. */ ,
per_cikis_neden AS [#msg_S_0759] /* ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ */ ,
per_muh_kod AS [#msg_S_0760] /* MUH.KODU */ ,
per_kim_meslek AS [#msg_S_0761] /* MESLEK */ ,
IsNull(per_dept_kod  + (select case when pdp_adi is not null Then ' / '+pdp_adi End
from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod),'') AS [#msg_S_0513] /* DEPARTMAN */ ,
IsNull(per_bolge_kodu + (select case when pbl_bolge_adi is not null Then ' / '+pbl_bolge_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI WITH (NOLOCK) where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu),'') AS [#msg_S_0514] /* BÖLGE */ ,
IsNull(per_kim_gorev + (select case when pgk_gorev_adi is not null Then ' / '+pgk_gorev_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev),'') AS [#msg_S_0515] /* GÖREV */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_nuf_dogum_tarih) AS [#msg_S_0762] /* DOĞ.TAR. */ ,
per_nuf_dogum_yer AS [#msg_S_0763] /* DOĞ.YERİ */ ,
per_ozel_not AS [#msg_S_0451] /* ÖZEL NOT */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_Kidem_Tarih) AS [#msg_S_0764] /* KIDEM TAR. */ ,
per_asgari_ucretli AS [#msg_S_0765] /* ASGARİ ÜCT. */ ,
Per_TcKimlikNo AS [#msg_S_0766] /* T.C.KİMLİK NO */ ,
Per_PersMailAddress AS [#msg_S_0767] /* E-POSTA ADR. */ ,
Per_Muh_Grup_Kodu AS [#msg_S_0768] /* MUHTASAR GRUP KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PersAktifCalismaKodu (per_kod) AS [#msg_S_2504] /* AKTİF ÇALIŞMA KODU */ ,
CASE WHEN per_Brut_net = 0 THEN 'Brütten nete' ELSE 'Netten brüte' END AS [#msg_S_0769] /* ÜCRET TİPİ */ ,
case when per_ucr_bode_yapilma = 1 then 'YAPILSIN' else 'YAPILMASIN' end AS [#msg_S_0770] /* BANK.ÖDEME */ ,
per_ucr_hesapno AS [#msg_S_0771] /* HESAP NO */ ,
(select ssk_maasbankakodu from dbo.PERSONEL_SSK_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where ssk_Sira_No = per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [#msg_S_0772] /* SSK BANKALAR */ ,
SGKBTipIsim AS [#msg_S_4458], /*TABİ OLDUĞU SGK BELGE TÜRÜ*/
SGKKanunNoVeIsim AS [#msg_S_4459], /*TABİ OLDUĞU SGK KANUNU*/
MKTipIsim AS [#msg_S_4460],/*TABİ OLDUĞU MALİYE KANUNU*/
per_special1 AS [#msg_S_0773] /* ÖZEL ALAN 1 */ ,
per_special2 AS [#msg_S_0774] /* ÖZEL ALAN 2 */ ,
per_special3 AS [#msg_S_0775] /* ÖZEL ALAN 3 */
FROM dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_SGK_Belge_Isimleri ON SGKBTipNo=per_sskbelge_turu
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_SGK_Kanun_Isimleri ON SGKKTipNo=per_tabiioldugukanun
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Maliye_Kanun_Isimleri ON MKTipNo=per_tabiioldugukanun2
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_TahakkukYonetim]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_TahakkukYonetim](@tah_yil int,
@tah_ay int, -- giriş çıkış tarihi kontrolü için
@tah_no int,
@ilkkod nvarchar(30),
@sonkod nvarchar(30),
@kodyapi nvarchar(30),
@SiralamaSekli tinyint,
@izleme bit =0,
@tah_aystr nvarchar(MAX) = '' ,
@tah_nostr nvarchar(500) = '')
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
pt_Guid           AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
per_Guid          AS [msg_S_0777] /* PKAYIT NO */ ,
PD.*,
pt_maliyil         AS [#msg_S_0517] /* MALİ YIL */ ,
pt_tah_ay          AS [#msg_S_1128] /* TAHAKKUK AYI */ ,
dbo.fn_AyIsimBul(pt_tah_ay) AS [msg_S_0778] /* TAH. AYI */ ,
pt_tahno           AS [#msg_S_0779] /* TAH. NO */ ,
case when (pt_tahno is null) or (pt_tahno = 0)
then RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',473,1,DEFAULT)) /* YOK */
else RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',473,2,DEFAULT)) /* VAR' */
end AS [msg_S_0780] /* PUANTAJ */ ,
case when (pt_kesin is null) or (pt_kesin = 0)
then RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',473,1,DEFAULT)) /* YOK */
else RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',473,2,DEFAULT))
end AS [msg_S_0781] /* KESİNLEŞTİRME */ ,
pt_sskgunu         AS [msg_S_0647] /* SSK GÜN */ ,
(pt_kazanc1_tksaat+pt_kazanc2_tksaat+pt_kazanc3_tksaat+pt_kazanc4_tksaat+pt_kazanc5_tksaat+
pt_kazanc6_tksaat)AS [msg_S_0599] /* SAAT */ ,
ISNULL(pt_normalkazanc,0) AS [msg_S_0624] /* KAZANÇ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_sskbrut,0) AS [msg_S_0648] /* SSK MATRAHI */ ,
ISNULL(pt_net,0)     AS [msg_S_0646] /* NET */ ,
ISNULL(pt_asgarigecimindirimi,0)AS [msg_S_3148] /* AGİ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_ilave_agi,0)AS [msg_S_4418] /* İLAVE EDİLEN AGİ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_sskprimi,0) AS [#msg_S_0634] /* SSK PRİMİ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_gvbrut,0)   AS [#msg_S_0650] /* GV MATRAH */ ,
ISNULL(pt_dv,0)       AS [#msg_S_0636] /* DAMGA VERGİSİ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_ekkazanc,0) AS [#msg_S_0625] /* EK KAZANÇ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_sosyrdm,0)  AS [#msg_S_0626] /* SOSYAL YARDIM */ ,
ISNULL(pt_kesinti,0)  AS [#msg_S_0643] /* TOPLAM KESİNTİ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_gv,0)       AS [#msg_S_0635] /* GELİR VERGİSİ */ ,
pt_izingunu           AS [#msg_S_0653] /* İZİN GÜNÜ */ ,
ISNULL(pt_izinmatrah,0) AS [#msg_S_0654] /* SSK İZİN MATRAH */ ,
ISNULL(pt_iszlksigperpayi,0) AS [#msg_S_0640] /* İŞS.SİG.PER.PAYI */ ,
ISNULL(pt_iszlksigisvpayi,0) AS [#msg_S_0641] /* İŞS.SİG.İŞV.PAYI */ ,
pt_EksikCalismaNedeni AS [#msg_S_0782] /* EKSİK ÇALIŞMA NEDENİ */ ,
dbo.fn_PerEksikGunNeden(pt_eksikcalismanedensecimli) AS [#msg_S_0783] /* EKSİK ÇALIŞMA NEDENİ(SEÇİMLİ) */,
IsNull(pt_DepartmanKodu  + (select case when pdp_adi is not null Then ' / '+pdp_adi End
from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu = pt_DepartmanKodu),'') AS [#msg_S_1790] /* PUANTAJ DEPARTMAN*/,
IsNull(pt_BolgeKodu + (select case when pbl_bolge_adi is not null Then ' / '+pbl_bolge_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI WITH (NOLOCK) where pbl_bolge_kodu = pt_BolgeKodu),'') AS [#msg_S_1791] /* PUANTAJ BÖLGE*/,
IsNull(pt_GorevKodu + (select case when pgk_gorev_adi is not null Then ' / '+pgk_gorev_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu = pt_GorevKodu),'') AS [#msg_S_1792] /* PUANTAJ GÖREV*/,
CASE WHEN pt_HesapTipi = 0
THEN RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,1,DEFAULT)) /* Brütten nete */
ELSE RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,2,DEFAULT)) /* Netten brüte */
END AS [#msg_S_1793] /* PUANTAJ MAAŞ TİPİ*/,
pt_brutucret AS [#msg_S_1794] /*PUANTAJ MAAŞI*/,
pt_otobes_tutari AS [msg_S_4425], /*OTOMATİK BES TUTARI*/
SGKBTipIsim      AS [#msg_S_4455], /*PUANTAJ SGK BELGE TÜRÜ*/
SGKKanunNoVeIsim AS [#msg_S_4456], /*PUANTAJ SGK KANUNU*/
MKTipIsim        AS [#msg_S_4457] /*PUANTAJ MALİYE KANUNU*/
FROM dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI WITH (NOLOCK) ON (per_kod=pt_pkod) and (pt_maliyil=@tah_yil) and
( (@izleme = 1) OR ((@izleme = 0) AND (pt_tah_ay=@tah_ay) AND (pt_tahno=@tah_no)) )
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.PERSDETAY_gizli PD ON (dbo.PERSONELLER.per_kod=PD.[msg_S_0078] /* KODU */ )
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_SGK_Belge_Isimleri ON SGKBTipNo=pt_tabiioldugubelgeturu
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_SGK_Kanun_Isimleri ON SGKKTipNo=pt_tabiioldugukanun
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Maliye_Kanun_Isimleri ON MKTipNo=pt_tabiioldugukanun2
WHERE ( (@izleme = 0) OR
( (@izleme = 1) AND (dbo.fn_abs_no_ok(pt_tah_ay,@tah_aystr)=1) AND (dbo.fn_abs_no_ok(pt_tahno,@tah_nostr)=1) )
)  AND
(dbo.fn_PersOk(@tah_yil,@tah_ay,per_giris_tar,per_cikis_tar) = 1) AND
(
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 1 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(dbo.fn_guid_to_str(per_Guid),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 2 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 3 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_adi,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 4 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_soyadi,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 5 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_sicil_no,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 6 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_dept_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 7 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_kim_gorev_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 8 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_nuf_seri_no,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 9 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_bolge_kodu,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli =10 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(cast(per_firma_no as nvarchar(30)),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli =13 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(cast(per_ucr_PSSK_sube as nvarchar(30)),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) )
)
ORDER BY [msg_S_0780] /* PUANTAJ */ ,
[msg_S_0781] /* KESİNLEŞTİRME */ ,
pt_pkod
)
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSONELLER_YONETIM]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[PERSONELLER_YONETIM]
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT
per_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
per_kod AS [msg_S_0078],
per_adi AS [msg_S_0870],
per_soyadi AS [msg_S_1040],
per_sicil_no AS [msg_S_1210] /* SSK SİCİLNO */ ,
per_dept_kod AS [msg_S_0513],
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_giris_tar) AS [msg_S_1211] /* GİRİŞ TARİHİ */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(per_cikis_tar) AS [msg_S_1065] /* ÇIKIŞ TARİHİ */ ,
per_cikis_neden AS  [#msg_S_0759] /* ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',767, DEFAULT), per_CikisSebebiSecimli+1, DEFAULT)    AS [#msg_S_1641] /*ÇIKIŞ NEDENİ(SEÇİMLİ)*/,
per_muh_kod AS [msg_S_1027] /* MUH. KODU */ ,
ssk_ismi AS [msg_S_0621] /* SSK ŞUBESİ */,
per_dept_kod AS [msg_S_0756] /* DEP.KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PerIsGrubu(per_is_grup) AS [msg_S_0622] /* İŞ GRUBU */ ,
per_kim_meslek AS [msg_S_0761] /* MESLEK */ ,
per_dept_kod AS [#msg_S_0871] /* DEPARTMAN KODU */,
(Select pdp_adi from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod) AS [#msg_S_0872] /* DEPARTMAN ADI*/ ,
per_bolge_kodu AS [#msg_S_1036] /* BÖLGE KODU */ ,
(select pbl_bolge_adi from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu) AS [#msg_S_1177] /* BÖLGE ADI*/ ,
per_kim_gorev AS [#msg_S_1700] /* GÖREV KODU */ ,
(select pgk_gorev_adi from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev) AS [#msg_S_0898] /* GÖREV ADI*/
FROM    dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_SSK_TANIMLARI ON ssk_Sira_No=per_ucr_PSSK_sube
ORDER BY per_kod
GO

CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_UcretSimulatoruIzleme](@yil integer,@aylar nvarchar(max))
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT
TOP 100 PERCENT
pt_pkod AS [msg_S_0501] /* PERSONEL KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,pt_pkod) AS [msg_S_0502] /* PERSONEL ADI */ ,
dbo.fn_SSK_Adi(per_ucr_PSSK_sube) AS [msg_S_0621] /* SSK ŞUBESİ */ ,
dbo.fn_PerIsGrubu(per_is_grup) AS [#msg_S_0622] /* İŞ GRUBU */ ,
IsNull(per_dept_kod  + (select case when pdp_adi is not null Then ' / '+pdp_adi End
from dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod),'') AS [msg_S_0513] /* DEPARTMAN */ ,
IsNull(per_bolge_kodu + (select case when pbl_bolge_adi is not null Then ' / '+pbl_bolge_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI WITH (NOLOCK) where pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu),'') AS [#msg_S_0514] /* BÖLGE */ ,
IsNull(per_kim_gorev + (select case when pgk_gorev_adi is not null Then ' / '+pgk_gorev_adi End
from dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev),'') AS [#msg_S_0515] /* GÖREV */ ,
per_muh_kod AS [msg_S_1027] /* MUH. KODU */ ,
per_kim_meslek AS [#msg_S_0761] /* MESLEK */ ,
Per_TcKimlikNo AS [msg_S_0766] /* T.C.KİMLİK NO */ ,
Per_PersMailAddress AS [#msg_S_0767] /* E-POSTA ADR. */ ,
CASE WHEN per_Brut_net = 0
THEN RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,1,DEFAULT)) /* Brütten nete */
ELSE RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',449,2,DEFAULT)) /* Netten brüte */
END AS [#msg_S_0769] /* ÜCRET TİPİ */ ,
CASE WHEN per_ucr_bode_yapilma = 0
THEN RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',472,1,DEFAULT)) /* Yapılmasın */
ELSE RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit('A',472,2,DEFAULT)) /* Yapılsın */
END AS [#msg_S_0770] /* BANK.ÖDEME */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',221, DEFAULT), per_tip+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_0077] /* TİPİ */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',466, DEFAULT), per_kim_tahsil+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1590]/* TAHSİLİ*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',470, DEFAULT), per_kim_sakat_derece+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1592] /*SAKATLIK DERECESİ*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',474, DEFAULT), per_kim_gocmen+1, DEFAULT)       AS [#msg_S_1593] /*GÖÇMEN KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',468, DEFAULT), per_kim_gorev_kod+1, DEFAULT)    AS [#msg_S_0897] /*GÖREV KODU*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',469, DEFAULT), per_kim_SGK_kod+1, DEFAULT)      AS [#msg_S_1594] /*SGK KODU*/,
per_ucr_send_durum            AS [#msg_S_1605] /*SENDİKA DURUMU*/,
per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr          AS [#msg_S_1607] /*SİGORTA % GRUBU*/,
per_ucr_vdaire                AS [#msg_S_0881] /*VERGİ DAİRESİ */,
per_ucr_konutfon              AS [#msg_S_1380] /*KONUT FONU        */,
per_ucr_onceod                AS [#msg_S_1610] /*ÖNCE ÖDM. KF. AYI             */,
per_yard_yol                  AS [#msg_S_1611] /*YOL YARIDMI           */,
per_yard_yemek                AS [#msg_S_1612] /*YEMEK YARDIMI         */,
per_yard_yakacak              AS [#msg_S_1613] /*YAKACAK YARDIMI          */,
per_yard_bayram               AS [#msg_S_1614] /*BAYRAM YARDIMI*/,
per_yard_cocuk                AS [#msg_S_1615] /*COCUK YARIDIMI*/,
per_yard_aile                 AS [#msg_S_1616] /*AİLE YARDIMI*/,
per_yard_ozelindirim          AS [#msg_S_1617] /*ÖZEL İNDRİM*/,
per_doviz_cinsi               AS [#msg_S_0849] /*DÖVİZ CİNSİ*/,
per_VkfKesOd_fl               AS [#msg_S_1620] /*VAKIF KESİNTİSİ UYGULANDI	*/,
per_iszlksig                  AS [#msg_S_1622] /*İŞSİZLİK SİGORTASI        */,
per_Calismatipi               AS [#msg_S_1623] /*ÇALIŞMA TİPİ              */,
per_mevsim                    AS [#msg_S_1624] /*ÇALIŞMA DÖNEMİ            */,
per_tabiioldugukanun          AS [#msg_S_1629] /*TABİİ OLDUĞU KANUN        */,
per_IdariAmirKodu             AS [#msg_S_1626] /*İDARİ AMİR KODU           */,
per_TeknikAmirKodu            AS [#msg_S_1627] /*TEKNİK AMİR KODU          */,
pt_maliyil             AS [msg_S_0517] /* MALİ YIL */ ,
cast(REPLACE(STR(pt_tah_ay,2,0), ' ', '0') + '.' + dbo.fn_AyIsimBul(pt_tah_ay) as nvarchar(20)) AS [msg_S_0223] /* AY */ ,
pt_tah_ay AS [#msg_S_1128] /* TAHAKKUK AYI */ ,
CAST(pt_tahno  AS nvarchar) AS [msg_S_0623] /* PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI NO */ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1602, DEFAULT), per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1963]/*BAĞLI SRM MERKEZİ */ ,
CASE  per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip
WHEN 1 THEN per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu+' '+dbo.fn_SorumlulukMerkeziIsmi(per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu)
WHEN 2 THEN per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu+' '+(Select top 1 dan_ismi FROM dbo.DAGITIM_ANAHTARI_TANIMLARI  WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu=dan_kod)
ELSE null
END AS [msg_S_1962] /*SRM.MRK Veya DAĞ.ANAH*/,
SUM(pt_normalkazanc)   AS [msg_S_0624] /* KAZANÇ */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc1_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi1_01] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc2_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi2_02] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc3_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi3_03] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc4_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi4_04] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc5_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi5_05] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_kazanc6_tktutar)AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kazanc_aciklamasi6_06] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ekkazanc)       AS [msg_S_0625] /* EK KAZANÇ */ ,
SUM(pt_ekkazanc1_tktutar)  AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_ek_kazanc_aciklamasi1_01] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ekkazanc2_tktutar)  AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_ek_kazanc_aciklamasi2_02] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ekkazanc3_tktutar)  AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_ek_kazanc_aciklamasi3_03] /* */ ,

SUM(pt_ozksnt13)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi13_13] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt14)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi14_14] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt15)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi15_15] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt16)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi16_16] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt17)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi17_17] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt18)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi18_18] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt19)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi19_19] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt20)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi20_20] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt21)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi21_21] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt22)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi22_22] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt23)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi23_23] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_ozksnt24)      AS [#tbl_0207_ysl_kesinti_aciklamasi24_24] /* */ ,
SUM(pt_iszlksigperpayi)AS [msg_S_0640] /* İŞS.SİG.PER.PAYI */ ,
SUM(pt_iszlksigisvpayi)AS [msg_S_0641] /* İŞS.SİG.İŞV.PAYI */ ,
SUM(pt_kesinti)        AS [msg_S_0643] /* TOPLAM KESİNTİ */ ,
SUM(pt_tersbakiye)     AS [msg_S_0644] /* TERS BAKİYE */ ,
SUM(pt_yuvfarki)       AS [msg_S_0645] /* YUVARLAMA FARKI */ ,
SUM(pt_asgarigecimindirimi)AS [msg_S_3148] /* AGİ */ ,
SUM(pt_net)            AS [msg_S_0646] /* NET */ ,
(SELECT sum(ISNULL(pt_net,0.0)) FROM dbo.PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI PT
WHERE (PT.pt_pkod=PTS.pt_pkod) and (PT.pt_maliyil=PTS.pt_maliyil) and (PT.pt_tah_ay=PTS.pt_tah_ay)) AS [#msg_S_2992], /*GERÇEKLEŞEN NET ÜCRET*/
CAST(SUM(pt_sskgunu) AS float) AS [msg_S_0647] /* SSK GÜN */ ,
SUM(pt_sskbrutmatrah)  AS [msg_S_0648] /* SSK MATRAHI */ ,
SUM(pt_devsskmatrah)   AS [msg_S_0649] /* DEV.SSK.MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_gvbrut)         AS [msg_S_0650] /* GV MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_gvmatrah)       AS [msg_S_0651] /* TOPLAM GV MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_devgvmatrah)    AS [msg_S_0652] /* DEV.GV.MATRAH */ ,
CAST(SUM(pt_izingunu) AS float) AS [#msg_S_0653] /* İZİN GÜNÜ */ ,
SUM(pt_izinmatrah)     AS [#msg_S_0654] /* SSK İZİN MATRAH */ ,
SUM(pt_sskisvhis)      AS [msg_S_0655] /* SSK İŞV.HİSSESİ */ ,
SUM(pt_sskkonfon)      AS [#msg_S_0656] /* SSK KONUT FONU */ ,
SUM(pt_digersigorta_isveren)   AS [msg_S_0642] /* DİĞER SİG.İND.İŞV */ ,
SUM(pt_digersigorta_calisan)   AS [msg_S_0665] /* DİĞER SİG.İND.ÇLŞ */ ,
SUM(pt_bireyselsigorta_isveren)AS [msg_S_0657] /* BİREYSEL SİG.İND.İŞV */,
SUM(pt_bireyselsigorta_calisan)AS [msg_S_1470] /* BİREYSEL SİG.İND.ÇLŞ */,
SUM(pt_kazanc+pt_sskisvhis+pt_iszlksigisvpayi) AS [msg_S_4196] /*İŞVEREN MALİYETİ*/
FROM dbo.PERSONEL_TAHAKKUKLARI_SIMULATOR PTS WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK) ON ( per_kod = pt_pkod )
WHERE (pt_maliyil=@yil) and (dbo.fn_no_ok(pt_tah_ay,@aylar)=1)
GROUP BY pt_maliyil,pt_tah_ay,pt_pkod,per_ucr_PSSK_sube,per_is_grup,pt_tahno,per_dept_kod,per_bolge_kodu,per_kim_gorev,
per_muh_kod,per_kim_meslek ,Per_TcKimlikNo,Per_PersMailAddress,per_Brut_net,per_ucr_bode_yapilma,per_tip,per_kim_tahsil,
per_kim_gocmen,per_kim_gorev_kod,per_kim_SGK_kod,per_ucr_send_durum,per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr,per_ucr_vdaire,
per_ucr_konutfon,per_ucr_onceod,per_yard_yol,per_yard_yemek,per_yard_yakacak,per_yard_bayram,
per_yard_cocuk,per_yard_aile,per_yard_ozelindirim,per_doviz_cinsi,per_VkfKesOd_fl,per_iszlksig,
per_Calismatipi,per_mevsim,per_tabiioldugukanun,per_IdariAmirKodu,per_TeknikAmirKodu,per_kim_sakat_derece,
per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip,per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu
ORDER BY  pt_maliyil,pt_tah_ay,pt_pkod,per_ucr_PSSK_sube,per_is_grup,pt_tahno,per_dept_kod,per_bolge_kodu,per_kim_gorev,
per_muh_kod,per_kim_meslek ,Per_TcKimlikNo,Per_PersMailAddress,per_Brut_net,per_ucr_bode_yapilma,per_tip,per_kim_tahsil,
per_kim_gocmen,per_kim_gorev_kod,per_kim_SGK_kod,per_ucr_send_durum,per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr,per_ucr_vdaire,
per_ucr_konutfon,per_ucr_onceod,per_yard_yol,per_yard_yemek,per_yard_yakacak,per_yard_bayram,
per_yard_cocuk,per_yard_aile,per_yard_ozelindirim,per_doviz_cinsi,per_VkfKesOd_fl,per_iszlksig,
per_Calismatipi,per_mevsim,per_tabiioldugukanun,per_IdariAmirKodu,per_TeknikAmirKodu,per_kim_sakat_derece,
per_srmmrkbaglanti_tip,per_srmmrkdaganah_kodu
)
GO

per_kim_lise                  AS [#msg_S_1598] /*ÇOCUK AD(LİSE)*/,

dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',477,DEFAULT), per_ucr_send_durum+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1605] /*SENDİKA DURUMU*/,
per_ucr_send                  AS [#msg_S_1606] /*SENDİKA*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',469,DEFAULT), per_ucr_sig_yuzde_gr+1, DEFAULT) AS [#msg_S_1607] /*SİGORTA % GRUBU*/,

per_ucr_onceod                AS [#msg_S_1610] /*ÖNCE ÖDM. KF. AYI             */,

per_VkfKesOd_fl               AS [#msg_S_1620] /*VAKIF KESİNTİSİ UYGULANDI	*/,
dbo.fn_EvetHayir(per_iszlksig)                  AS [#msg_S_1622] /*İŞSİZLİK SİGORTASI        */,

per_IdariAmirKodu             AS [#msg_S_1626] /*İDARİ AMİR KODU           */,
per_TeknikAmirKodu            AS [#msg_S_1627] /*TEKNİK AMİR KODU          */,
per_ilksoyad                  AS [#msg_S_1628] /*İLK SOYAD                 */,
per_boyu                      AS [#msg_S_1630] /*BOYU                      */,
per_kilo                      AS [#msg_S_1631] /*KİLOSU                    */,
per_gomlek_bed                AS [#msg_S_1632] /*GÖMLEK BEDENİ             */,
per_pant_bed                  AS [#msg_S_1633] /*PANTLON BEDENİ            */,
per_etek_bed                  AS [#msg_S_1634] /*ETEK BEDENİ               */,
per_ayak_no                   AS [#msg_S_1635] /*AYAKKABI NO               */,
per_sapka_bed                 AS [#msg_S_1636] /*SAPKA BEDENİ              */,
per_onluk_bed                 AS [#msg_S_1637] /*ÖNLÜK BEDENİ              */,
per_diger_bed1                AS [#msg_S_1638] /*DİĞER BEDENİ 1            */,
per_diger_bed2                AS [#msg_S_1639] /*DİĞER BEDENİ 2            */,
per_diger_bed3                AS [#msg_S_1640]/*DİĞER BEDENİ 3            */,
per_special1                  AS [#msg_S_0773] /* ÖZEL ALAN 1 */ ,

per_special3                  AS [#msg_S_0775] /* ÖZEL ALAN 3 */
FROM dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_SSK_TANIMLARI ON ssk_Sira_No=per_ucr_PSSK_sube
WHERE 	  ( ( @SiralamaSekli = 1 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(dbo.fn_guid_to_str (per_Guid),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 2 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 3 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_adi,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 4 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_soyadi,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 5 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_sicil_no,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 6 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_dept_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 7 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_kim_gorev_kod,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 8 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_nuf_seri_no,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli = 9 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(per_bolge_kodu,@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,0)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli =10 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(cast(per_firma_no as nvarchar(30)),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) ) OR
( ( @SiralamaSekli =13 ) AND (dbo.fn_PersKodOk(cast(per_ucr_PSSK_sube as nvarchar(30)),@ilkkod,@sonkod,@kodyapi,1)=1) )
ORDER BY per_kod )
GO

 CONSTRAINT [NDX_PERSONEL_TALEPLERI_00] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED

CREATE VIEW [dbo].[ELEMANTALEP_YONETIM]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
tlp_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
tlp_kodu  AS [msg_S_0078] /* KODU */,
tlp_adi  AS [msg_S_0870] /* ADI */ ,
tlp_tarih  AS [msg_S_1695]/*TALEP TARİHİ*/,
tlp_bitistarih  AS [msg_S_0265]/* BİTİŞ TARİHİ*/,
tlp_grv_kodu AS [msg_S_0897]/* GÖREV KODU*/,
(Select pgk_gorev_adi from PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) where pgk_gorev_kodu=tlp_grv_kodu) AS [msg_S_0898]/* GÖREV ADI*/  ,
tlp_dpt_kodu AS [msg_S_0871]/* DEPARTMAN KODU*/,
(Select pdp_adi from DEPARTMANLAR WITH (NOLOCK) where pdp_kodu=tlp_dpt_kodu) AS [msg_S_0872]/* DEPARTMAN ADI*/,
tlp_eden_per_kodu AS [msg_S_2631]/* TALEP EDEN PERSONEL */ ,
tlp_adet  AS [msg_S_2632] /*TALEP ADEDİ*/,
tlp_durum AS [msg_S_1696] /* TALEP DURUMU*/ ,
tlp_aciklama1 AS [msg_S_1007] /*GENEL AÇIKLAMA 1*/ ,
tlp_aciklama2  AS [msg_S_1009]/* GENEL AÇIKLAMA 2*/ ,
tlp_aciklama3  AS [msg_S_1010]/* GENEL AÇIKLAMA 3*/ ,
tlp_aciklama4   AS [msg_S_1011]/* GENEL AÇIKLAMA4*/ ,
tlp_aciklama5   AS [msg_S_1012]/* GENEL AÇIKLAMA 5*/ ,
tlp_kadro_kodu  AS [msg_S_2900] /* KADRO KODU*/ ,
TEP.per_sicil_no AS [msg_S_1066] /* SİCİL NO */ ,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,TEP.per_kod) AS [msg_S_1250] /* ADI SOYADI */ ,
TEP.per_kim_gorev_kod AS [msg_S_1067] /*PERSONEL GÖREVİ*/,
(SELECT pgk_gorev_adi FROM dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WHERE pgk_gorev_kodu=TEP.per_kim_gorev) AS [msg_S_1251] /* GÖREVİ */ ,
TEP.per_Isy_KimlikNo AS [#ID],
TEP.Per_PersMailAddress AS  [msg_S_1038] /* E-POSTA ADRESİ*/,
TEP.per_IdariAmirKodu AS [msg_S_2967] /* İDARI AMİR KADRO KODU*/,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,TEP.per_IdariAmirKodu)  AS [msg_S_2968] /* İDARI AMİR KADRO ACIKLAMA*/,
TEP.per_TeknikAmirKodu AS [msg_S_2969] /* TEKNİK AMİR KADRO KODU*/,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,TEP.per_TeknikAmirKodu)   AS [msg_S_2970] /* TEKNİK AMİR KADRO ACIKLAMA*/,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('T',4518,DEFAULT),tlp_nedeni+1,DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_0317]/* NEDEN*/ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('T',4519,DEFAULT),tlp_cinsiyet+1,DEFAULT)[msg_S_1258],/* CİNSİYETİ*/
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('T',4520,DEFAULT),tlp_medeni_hal+1,DEFAULT)AS [msg_S_1601]/* MEDENİ HAL*/,
tlp_minyas     AS [msg_S_4190]/*Min YAŞ*/   ,
tlp_maxyas     AS [msg_S_4191]/*Max YAŞ*/   ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('T',4521,DEFAULT),tlp_askerlik+1,DEFAULT)   AS [msg_S_2002] /* ASKERLİK DURUMU*/ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1292,DEFAULT),tlp_ehliyet+1,DEFAULT)   AS [msg_S_4189]/*EHLİYET*/ ,
tlp_tecrube  AS [msg_S_4192]/*TECRÜBE*/     ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',467,DEFAULT),tlp_dil_tipi+1,DEFAULT)   AS [msg_S_4193]/*DİL*/ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1290,DEFAULT),tlp_dil_seviye+1,DEFAULT) AS [msg_S_4194]/*OKUMA/YAZMA*/   ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1290,DEFAULT),tlp_dil_konusma+1,DEFAULT)AS [msg_S_4195]/*KONUŞMA*/ ,
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',470,DEFAULT),tlp_ozurderecesi +1,DEFAULT)  AS [msg_S_2013],
dbo.fn_Split(dbo.fn_GetResourceMax('A',1640,DEFAULT),tlp_ozurgrubu +1,DEFAULT)  AS [msg_S_2014]
FROM dbo.PERSONEL_TALEPLERI WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN dbo.PERSONELLER TEP WITH (NOLOCK) ON ( per_kod = tlp_eden_per_kodu )
ORDER BY tlp_kodu
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_EgitimOperasyonu]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_EgitimOperasyonu](@ilktar  datetime,
@sontar  datetime,
@durum     tinyint,
@ilkkod  nvarchar(25),
@sonkod  nvarchar(25),
@kodyapi nvarchar(25),
@minegitim integer,
@maxegitim integer,
@minsinav integer,
@maxsinav integer )
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT
dbo.PERSONEL_ALINAN_EGITIMLER.aeg_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(dbo.PERSONEL_ALINAN_EGITIMLER.aeg_tarih) AS TARIH,
aeg_per_kodu AS [msg_S_0501] /* PERSONEL KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_PersFullName(7,aeg_per_kodu) AS [msg_S_0502] /* PERSONEL ADI */ ,
dbo.fn_EgitimTipi(egt_tipi) AS [msg_S_0503] /* EGITIM TIPI */ ,
aeg_egitim_kodu AS [msg_S_0506] /* EGITIM KODU */ ,
egt_adi AS [msg_S_0507] /* EGITIM ADI */ ,
dbo.fn_SecondsToDuration(egt_suresi)  AS [msg_S_0508] /* EGITIM SÜRESI */ ,
dbo.fn_EgitimDurumu(dbo.PERSONEL_ALINAN_EGITIMLER.aeg_durumu) AS [msg_S_0509] /* EGITIM DURUMU */ ,
egt_puan            AS [msg_S_2586] /*  EGITIMIN PUANI*/,
aeg_sinav_puan AS [msg_S_0510] /* ALINAN PUAN */ ,
CASE
When (aeg_sinav_puan>=egt_puan) and (aeg_durumu=1) then dbo.fn_GetResource('T',5,DEFAULT)
When (aeg_sinav_puan<egt_puan) and (aeg_durumu=1) then dbo.fn_GetResource('T',6,DEFAULT)
end AS [msg_S_0262]/* DURUM */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(aeg_bastar) AS [msg_S_0511] /* EGITIM TARIHI */ ,
aeg_aciklama1+' '+aeg_aciklama2+' '+aeg_aciklama3 AS [msg_S_0085] /* AÇIKLAMA */ ,
IsNull(per_dept_kod +(SELECT     CASE WHEN pdp_adi IS NOT NULL THEN ' / ' + pdp_adi END
FROM  dbo.DEPARTMANLAR    WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE      pdp_kodu = per_dept_kod), '') AS [msg_S_0513] /* DEPARTMAN */ ,
IsNull(per_bolge_kodu +(SELECT     CASE WHEN pbl_bolge_adi IS NOT NULL THEN ' / ' + pbl_bolge_adi END
FROM   dbo.PERSONEL_BOLGELERI   WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE      pbl_bolge_kodu = per_bolge_kodu), '') AS [msg_S_0514] /* BÖLGE */ ,
IsNull(per_kim_gorev + (SELECT     CASE WHEN pgk_gorev_adi IS NOT NULL THEN ' / ' + pgk_gorev_adi END
FROM    dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI        WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE      pgk_gorev_kodu = per_kim_gorev), '') AS [msg_S_0515] /* GÖREV */
FROM         dbo.PERSONEL_ALINAN_EGITIMLER WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN dbo.PERSONELLER WITH (NOLOCK) ON ( per_kod = aeg_per_kodu )
INNER JOIN dbo.PERSONEL_EGITIM_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) ON (egt_kodu = aeg_egitim_kodu)
WHERE   ((@durum = 3) or (@durum=aeg_durumu) )and
( ( (egt_kodu>=@ilkkod) or (@ilkkod='') ) and
( (egt_kodu<=@sonkod) or (@sonkod='') ) and
( (egt_kodu like @kodyapi+'%') or (@kodyapi='') ) )and
((@maxegitim=0) or( egt_puan between @minegitim and @maxegitim))and
((@maxsinav=0) or( aeg_sinav_puan between @minsinav and @maxsinav))and
((aeg_tarih>=@ilktar)or (@ilktar is NULL))and
((aeg_tarih <=@sontar)or (@sontar is NULL))
)
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSONEL_KIMLIK]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[PERSONEL_KIMLIK]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
dbo.PERSONELLER.per_sicil_no AS msg_S_1066, dbo.fn_PersFullName(7, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_kod) AS msg_S_1250,
(SELECT pdp_adi FROM dbo.DEPARTMANLAR WHERE (pdp_kodu = dbo.PERSONELLER.per_dept_kod)) AS msg_S_0513,
(SELECT pgk_gorev_adi FROM dbo.PERSONEL_GOREV_TANIMLARI WHERE (pgk_gorev_kodu = dbo.PERSONELLER.per_kim_gorev)) AS msg_S_1251,
dbo.mye_ImageData.Data AS msg_S_1252, dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(dbo.PERSONELLER.per_giris_tar) AS [#msg_S_1211],
dbo.PERSONELLER.per_Isy_KimlikNo AS [#ID], dbo.fn_KanGrubuBul(dbo.PERSONELLER.per_nuf_kangrup) AS msg_S_1602, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_Guid, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_kod, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_adi,
dbo.PERSONELLER.per_soyadi, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_sicil_no, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_dept_kod, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_kim_gorev, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_nuf_seri_no, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_bolge_kodu,
dbo.PERSONELLER.per_firma_no, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_cikis_tar, dbo.PERSONELLER.per_giris_tar
FROM dbo.PERSONELLER
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.mye_ImageData ON dbo.mye_ImageData.TableID = dbo.PERSONELLER.per_fileid AND dbo.mye_ImageData.Record_uid = dbo.PERSONELLER.per_Guid
WHERE (dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(dbo.PERSONELLER.per_cikis_tar) IS NULL)
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[PERSONEL_KADRO_EGITIMLERI_YONETIM]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[PERSONEL_KADRO_EGITIMLERI_YONETIM]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
ke_Guid  AS [#msg_S_0088], -- KAYIT NO
ke_kadrokod    AS [msg_S_2900],/* KADRO KODU */
ISNULL((SELECT kdr_aciklama FROM dbo.PERSONEL_KADRO_TANIMLARI WHERE kdr_kod=ke_kadrokod),'') AS [msg_S_2901],  /* KADRO AÇIKLAMASI */
ke_kadrosirano   AS [msg_S_0157], /* SIRA NO */
ke_satirno AS [msg_S_0212], /* SATIR NO */
ke_egitimkod AS [msg_S_0506],/* EĞİTİM KODU */
CASE WHEN ke_tipi = 0 THEN ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 egt_adi FROM dbo.PERSONEL_EGITIM_TANIMLARI WHERE egt_kodu=ke_egitimkod),'')
ELSE ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 egr_adi FROM dbo.EGITIM_GRUP_TANIMLARI WHERE egr_kod=ke_egitimkod),'')
END AS [msg_S_0507]/* EĞİTİM ADI */
FROM dbo.PERSONEL_KADRO_EGITIMLERI WITH (NOLOCK)
ORDER BY ke_kadrokod,ke_kadrosirano,ke_satirno
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_KiraSozlesmesiOperasyon]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_KiraSozlesmesiOperasyon]
(@OpTipi    tinyint = 0,
@ilktar   datetime = NULL,
@sontar  datetime = NULL,
@TarihTipi tinyint = 0,    -- {0:Kira başl.tarihi   1:Kira bitiş tarihi 2:Sözleşme tarihi 3:Yer tesl.tarihi }
@onayli tinyint = 0,       -- {0:Onaysiz       1:Onayli       2:hepsi          }
@sozlesmeli tinyint = 0    -- {0:Hepsi         1:sözleşmesi oluşmamış olanlar          }
)
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
Avmk_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
Avmk_kira_kodu AS [msg_S_4049] /* KİRA KODU */ ,
Avmk_kira_ismi AS [msg_S_4050] /* KİRA İSMİ */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(Avmk_baslangictarihi) AS [msg_S_0264] /* BAŞLAMA TARİHİ */ ,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(Avmk_bitistarihi) AS [msg_S_0265] /* BİTİŞ TARİHİ */,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(Avmk_sozlesmetarihi) AS [msg_S_2756] /* SÖZLEŞME TARİHİ */,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(Avmk_yertestarihi) AS [msg_S_2757] /* YER TESLİM TARİHİ */,
dbo.fn_DateTimeKontrol(Avmk_MagazaAcilisTarihi) AS [msg_S_3006] /* MAĞAZA AÇILIŞ TARİHİ */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('E',4384,Avmk_KiraTarHesSekli+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_3007]  /* KİRA TARİHİ HESAPLAMA ŞEKLİ */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3977,Avmk_kirayontemi+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_2758]  /* KİRA YÖNTEMİ */,
Avmk_pesinkira AS [msg_S_2753] /* PEŞİN KİRA */,
dbo.fn_DovizIsmi(Avmk_dvzcinsi) AS [msg_S_0849] /* DÖVİZ CİNSİ */,
Avmk_brutalan  AS [msg_S_2754] /* BRÜT ALAN */,
Avmk_netalan   AS [msg_S_2755] /* NET ALAN */,
dbo.fn_EvetHayir(Avmk_cagrilabilir_fl) AS [msg_S_1734] /* ONAY */ ,
KULLANICI_KISA_ADI AS [msg_S_0256] /* ONAYLAYAN KULLANICI */,
dbo.fn_EvetHayir(Avmk_SozlesmeOlustu_fl) AS [msg_S_2752] /* HİZM.SAT.SÖZL. OLUŞTU */,
dbo.fn_KiraSozlesmesiCariBul(Avmk_kira_kodu) AS [msg_S_0200] /* CARİ KODU */ ,
Avmk_Kiratan1kirablmkodu  AS [msg_S_2839] /* KİRA 1.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
Avmk_Kiratan2kirablmkodu  AS [msg_S_2840] /* KİRA 2.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
Avmk_Kiratan3kirablmkodu  AS [msg_S_2841] /* KİRA 3.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
Avmk_Kiratan4kirablmkodu  AS [msg_S_2842] /* KİRA 4.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
Avmk_Kiratan5kirablmkodu  AS [msg_S_2843] /* KİRA 5.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
Avmk_OrtGidtan1OrtGidblmkodu  AS [msg_S_2844] /* ORT.GİD. 1.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3978,Avmk_OrtGidtan1OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_4019]  /* ORT.GİD. 1.ORT.ALANA KAT.ŞEKLİ */,
Avmk_OrtGidtan2OrtGidblmkodu  AS [msg_S_2845] /* ORT.GİD. 2.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3978,Avmk_OrtGidtan2OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_4020]  /* ORT.GİD. 2.ORT.ALANA KAT.ŞEKLİ */,
Avmk_OrtGidtan3OrtGidblmkodu  AS [msg_S_2846] /* ORT.GİD. 3.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3978,Avmk_OrtGidtan3OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_4021]  /* ORT.GİD. 3.ORT.ALANA KAT.ŞEKLİ */,
Avmk_OrtGidtan4OrtGidblmkodu  AS [msg_S_2847] /* ORT.GİD. 4.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3978,Avmk_OrtGidtan4OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_4022]  /* ORT.GİD. 4.ORT.ALANA KAT.ŞEKLİ */,
Avmk_OrtGidtan5OrtGidblmkodu  AS [msg_S_2848] /* ORT.GİD. 5.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3978,Avmk_OrtGidtan5OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_4023]  /* ORT.GİD. 5.ORT.ALANA KAT.ŞEKLİ */
FROM dbo.AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.KULLANICILAR_VIEW ON KULLANICI_NO=Avmk_OnaylayanKulNo
WHERE ( ( ((Avmk_baslangictarihi>=@ilktar) or (@ilktar is NULL)) AND
((Avmk_baslangictarihi<=@sontar) or (@sontar is NULL)) AND
(@TarihTipi=0)
) OR
(
((Avmk_bitistarihi>=@ilktar) or (@ilktar is NULL)) AND
((Avmk_bitistarihi<=@sontar) or (@sontar is NULL)) AND
(@TarihTipi=1)
) OR
(
((Avmk_sozlesmetarihi>=@ilktar) or (@ilktar is NULL)) AND
((Avmk_sozlesmetarihi<=@sontar) or (@sontar is NULL)) AND
(@TarihTipi=2)
) OR
(
((Avmk_yertestarihi>=@ilktar) or (@ilktar is NULL)) AND
((Avmk_yertestarihi<=@sontar) or (@sontar is NULL)) AND
(@TarihTipi=3)
)
) AND
( ((Avmk_OnaylayanKulNo=0) AND (@onayli=0)) OR ((Avmk_OnaylayanKulNo<>0) AND (@onayli=1)) OR (@onayli=2) ) AND
((@sozlesmeli=0) OR ( ((@sozlesmeli=1) AND (@OpTipi in (0,1)) AND (Avmk_SozlesmeOlustu_fl=0)) OR
((@sozlesmeli=1) AND (@OpTipi in (2)) AND (Avmk_SabitGiderSozlesmeOlustu_fl=0)) )  ) AND
(AvmkSozlesmeFeshedildi_fl=0) AND
( (@OpTipi<>2) OR ((@OpTipi=2) AND ((Avmk_OrtGidtan1OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl in (1,3)) or (Avmk_OrtGidtan2OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl in (1,3)) or
(Avmk_OrtGidtan3OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl in (1,3)) or (Avmk_OrtGidtan4OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl in (1,3)) or
(Avmk_OrtGidtan5OrtGidblmOrtakAlanKatSkl in (1,3))) ) ) AND
( (@OpTipi<>1) OR ((@OpTipi=1) AND (Avmk_kirayontemi in (0,2)) AND (Avmk_Malsahibi_fl=0)) )
ORDER BY Avmk_baslangictarihi
)
GO

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_AVMBolumKiraKubu]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_AVMBolumKiraKubu]()
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
blm_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
blm_sitekod AS [msg_S_2692] /*SİTE KODU*/,
blm_blokkod AS [msg_S_2694] /* BLOK KODU */ ,
blm_katkod AS [msg_S_2696] /* KAT KODU */,
blm_kod   AS [msg_S_2698] /* BÖLÜM KODU */ ,
blm_ismi  AS [msg_S_2699] /* BÖLÜM İSMİ */ ,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3974,blm_acikkapali+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_1155] /*AÇIK / KAPALI*/,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3975,blm_turu+1,DEFAULT))  AS [msg_S_3194] /* BÖLÜM TÜRÜ*/,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3984,blm_Cinsi+1,DEFAULT))  AS [msg_S_3195] /* BÖLÜM CİNSİ*/,
Avmk_kira_kodu AS [msg_S_4049]/* KİRA KODU*/,
Avmk_kira_ismi AS [msg_S_4050]/* KİRA İSMİ*/,
Avmk_baslangictarihi AS [msg_S_3196]/*KİRA BAŞLANGIÇ*/,
Avmk_bitistarihi AS [msg_S_3197]/*KİRA BİTİŞ*/,
datediff(day, getdate(), Avmk_bitistarihi) AS [msg_S_3198]/* BİTİME KALAN GÜN*/,
Avmk_srmrkkodu AS [msg_S_0137] /* SORUMLULUK MERKEZİ */ ,
Avmk_sektorkodu  AS [msg_S_1035] /* SEKTÖR KODU */ ,
Avmk_markakodu AS [msg_S_4563] /* MARKA KODU */ ,
Avmk_ProjeKodu AS [msg_S_0116] /* PROJE KODU */ ,
RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('A',3977,Avmk_kirayontemi+1,DEFAULT)) AS [msg_S_2758]  /* KİRA YÖNTEMİ */,
cari_unvan1 +' '+cari_unvan2 AS [msg_S_1033] /* CARI ÜNVANI */,
cari_sektor_kodu AS [msg_S_0474] /* CARİ SEKTÖR KODU */,
cari_bolge_kodu AS [msg_S_0473] /* BÖLGE KODU */,
cari_grup_kodu AS [msg_S_0471]  /* CARİ GRUP KODU */,
cari_temsilci_kodu AS [msg_S_0977] /* TEMSİLCİ KODU*/,
cari_wwwadresi AS [msg_S_3199] /*CARİ WWW*/,
cari_EMail AS [msg_S_0767] /* E-POSTA ADR.*/,
case when RTRIM(LTRIM(ISNULL(cari_kod ,'')))='' Then  RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('F',3091,3,DEFAULT)) Else RTrim(dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('F',3091,2,DEFAULT)) End AS  [msg_S_3200] /*BOŞ / DOLU*/,
blm_iccephe AS [msg_S_3191] /* İÇ ÇEPHE*/,
blm_discephe AS [msg_S_3192] /*  DIŞ CEPHE*/,
blm_vitrinsinifi AS [msg_S_3193] /*  VİTRİN*/,
blm_brutalan AS [msg_S_2754]/* BRÜT ALAN */ ,
blm_netalan AS [msg_S_2755] /* NET ALAN*/
FROM BAGIMSIZ_BOLUM_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI on
(((Avmk_Malsahibi_fl=0) And
((blm_kod = Avmk_Kiratan1kirablmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_Kiratan2kirablmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_Kiratan3kirablmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_Kiratan4kirablmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_Kiratan5kirablmkodu) ))
Or
((Avmk_Malsahibi_fl=1) And
((blm_kod = Avmk_OrtGidtan1OrtGidblmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_OrtGidtan2OrtGidblmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_OrtGidtan3OrtGidblmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_OrtGidtan4OrtGidblmkodu) or
(blm_kod = Avmk_OrtGidtan5OrtGidblmkodu) )
)
) And
(AvmkSozlesmeFeshedildi_fl=0) and
(Avmk_bitistarihi > getdate())
LEFT OUTER JOIN CARI_HESAPLAR on
((cari_AvmBilgileri1KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri2KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri3KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri4KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri5KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri6KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri7KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri8KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri9KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu) Or
(cari_AvmBilgileri10KiraKodu = Avmk_kira_kodu))
)
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI_CHOOSE_2]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI_CHOOSE_2]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
Avmk_Guid    AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
Avmk_kira_kodu  AS [msg_S_4049] /* SÖZLEŞME KODU */ ,
Avmk_kira_ismi  AS [msg_S_4050] /* SÖZLEŞME İSMİ */ ,
Avmk_markakodu AS [msg_S_4563] /* MARKA KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan1kirablmkodu
ELSE Avmk_OrtGidtan1OrtGidblmkodu
END AS [msg_S_3174] /* 1.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan2kirablmkodu
ELSE Avmk_OrtGidtan2OrtGidblmkodu
END AS [msg_S_3175] /* 2.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan3kirablmkodu
ELSE Avmk_OrtGidtan3OrtGidblmkodu
END AS [msg_S_3176] /* 3.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan4kirablmkodu
ELSE Avmk_OrtGidtan4OrtGidblmkodu
END AS [msg_S_3177] /* 4.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan5kirablmkodu
ELSE Avmk_OrtGidtan5OrtGidblmkodu
END AS [msg_S_3178] /* 5.BAĞIMSIZ ALAN  KODU */
FROM dbo.AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI
ORDER BY Avmk_kira_kodu
GO

Avmk_kira_kodu  AS [msg_S_4049] /* SÖZLEŞME KODU */ ,
Avmk_markakodu AS [msg_S_4563] /* MARKA KODU */ ,
CASE
WHEN Avmk_Malsahibi_fl = 0
THEN Avmk_Kiratan1kirablmkodu

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_CariHizmetSatisSozlesmesiOperasyonu]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_CariHizmetSatisSozlesmesiOperasyonu]
(
@ilktar datetime = NULL,
@sontar datetime = NULL,
@onayli tinyint = 0, -- {0:Onaysiz 1:Onayli 2:hepsi
@durumu tinyint = 0, -- {0:Faturalanmamış 1:Faturalanmış 2:hepsi
@TarihTipi tinyint = 0     -- {0: Evrak tarihi       1 : Sözleşme tarihi
)
RETURNS TABLE AS
RETURN
(
Select TOP 100 PERCENT
HSS_Guid AS [#msg_S_0088] /* KAYIT NO */ ,
HSS_evraktarihi AS [msg_S_0263] /* EVRAK TARİHİ */ ,
dbo.fn_EvrNoForm(HSS_evrakseri, HSS_evraksira) AS [msg_S_0327] /* EVRAK NO */ ,
HSS_belgeno As [msg_S_0093] /* BELGE NO */ ,
CASE
WHEN HSS_kesfatsira = 0 THEN dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('E',339, 1, DEFAULT)
ELSE dbo.fn_ResourceSplit ('E',339, 2, DEFAULT)
END AS [msg_S_0355] /* DURUMU */ ,
HSS_evraksatir AS [msg_S_0212] /* SATIR NO */ ,
CCinsIsim AS [msg_S_0199] /* CARİ CİNSİ */ ,
HSS_carikodu AS [msg_S_0200] /* CARİ KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_CarininIsminiBul (0,HSS_carikodu) AS [msg_S_0201] /* CARİ İSMİ */ ,
HSS_carisrmmrk AS [msg_S_0424] /* CARİ SORUMLULUK MERKEZİ */ ,
dbo.fn_SorumlulukMerkeziIsmi(HSS_carisrmmrk) AS [msg_S_0425] /* CARİ SORUMLULUK MERKEZİ ADI */ ,
HSS_tarihi AS [msg_S_0089] /* TARİH */ ,
HSS_hizmetkodu AS [msg_S_0427] /* HİZMET KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_CarininIsminiBul (3,HSS_hizmetkodu) AS [msg_S_0428] /* HİZMET İSMİ */ ,
HSS_aciklama AS [msg_S_0085] /* AÇIKLAMA */ ,
HSS_fiyati AS [msg_S_0006] /* FİYAT */ ,
HSS_miktari AS [msg_S_0165] /* MİKTAR */ ,
(HSS_fiyati *HSS_miktari ) AS [msg_S_0401] /* TOPLAM */ ,
dbo.fn_DovizSembolu(HSS_doviz_cins) AS [msg_S_0254] /* DÖVİZ */ ,
HSS_doviz_kur AS [msg_S_0302] /* DÖVİZ KURU */ ,
HSS_kesfatseri AS [msg_S_0429] /* KESİLEN FATURA SERİ */ ,
HSS_kesfatsira AS [msg_S_0430] /* KESİLEN FATURA SIRA NO */ ,
(select TOP 1 cha_tarihi from dbo.CARI_HESAP_HAREKETLERI WITH (NOLOCK)
where (cha_cinsi in (8,36)) AND
(cha_evrak_tip = 63 ) AND
(cha_normal_Iade = 0) AND
(cha_evrakno_seri = HSS_kesfatseri) AND
(cha_evrakno_sira = HSS_kesfatsira)) AS [msg_S_3171] /* KESİLEN FATURA TARİHİ */ ,
HSS_srmmrkkodu AS [msg_S_0137] /* SORUMLULUK MERKEZİ */ ,
dbo.fn_SorumlulukMerkeziIsmi(HSS_srmmrkkodu) AS [msg_S_0431] /* SORUMLULUK MERKEZİ ADI */ ,
HSS_projekodu AS [msg_S_0116] /* PROJE KODU */ ,
dbo.fn_ProjeIsmi(HSS_projekodu) AS [msg_S_0117] /* PROJE ADI */,
HSS_saticikodu AS [msg_S_1129] /* SORUMLU KODU */,
dbo.fn_CarininIsminiBul(1,HSS_saticikodu) AS [msg_S_1130] /* SORUMLU İSMİ */,
HSS_carisozlesmekodu AS [msg_S_1684], /* CARİ SÖZLEŞME KODU */
dbo.fn_AktivasyonAdi(HSS_carisozlesmeakttipi) AS [msg_S_1686], /* AKTİVASYON TİPİ */
HSS_carisozlesmeakttipi AS [#msg_S_1687] /* AKTİVASYON TİP NO*/,
HSS_BagliKiraKodu AS [#msg_S_4049] /* KİRA KODU */
FROM HIZMET_SATIS_SOZLESMELERI WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Cari_Cins_Isimleri ON CCinsNo=0
WHERE ( ( ((HSS_evraktarihi>=@ilktar) and (@TarihTipi=0)) or ((HSS_tarihi>=@ilktar) and (@TarihTipi=1)) ) OR (@ilktar is NULL)) AND
( ( ((HSS_evraktarihi<=@sontar) and (@TarihTipi=0)) or ((HSS_tarihi<=@sontar) and (@TarihTipi=1)) ) OR (@sontar is NULL)) AND
( (@durumu = 2) OR
((@durumu = 1) AND (HSS_kesfatsira <> 0)) OR
((@durumu = 0) AND (HSS_kesfatsira = 0)) ) AND
( ((HSS_OnaylayanKulNo=0) AND (@onayli=0)) OR ((HSS_OnaylayanKulNo<>0) AND (@onayli=1)) OR (@onayli=2) ) AND
((HSS_BagliKiraKodu='') OR ((HSS_BagliKiraKodu<>'') AND
((0=(SELECT AvmkSozlesmeFeshedildi_fl FROM dbo.AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE Avmk_kira_kodu=HSS_BagliKiraKodu)) OR
(HSS_tarihi<(SELECT AvmkSozlesmeFeshedilmeTarihi FROM dbo.AVMKIRA_TANIMLARI WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE Avmk_kira_kodu=HSS_BagliKiraKodu))) ) )
ORDER BY HSS_evraktarihi,HSS_evrakseri ,HSS_evraksira,HSS_evraksatir
)
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[STOK_HAREKETLERI_VIEW_WITH_INDEX_13_ISEMRI]    Script Date: 6/14/2024 1:56:48 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[STOK_HAREKETLERI_VIEW_WITH_INDEX_13_ISEMRI]
AS
SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT
SH.*,
SHEVRAK.SHEvrIsim,
SHCINS.SHCinsIsim,
SHTIP.SHTipIsim,
SHNI.NIIsim,
SHCARICINS.CCinsIsim,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_tutar,0,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_BRUT_DEGER_ANA,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_tutar,1,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_BRUT_DEGER_ALT,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_tutar,2,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_BRUT_DEGER_STOK_ORJ,
dbo.fn_StokHareketNetDeger(sth_tutar,
sth_iskonto1,sth_iskonto2,sth_iskonto3,sth_iskonto4,sth_iskonto5,sth_iskonto6,
sth_masraf1,sth_masraf2,sth_masraf3,sth_masraf4,
sth_otvtutari,sth_oivtutari,sth_tip,0,
sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_NET_DEGER_ANA,
dbo.fn_StokHareketNetDeger(sth_tutar,
sth_iskonto1,sth_iskonto2,sth_iskonto3,sth_iskonto4,sth_iskonto5,sth_iskonto6,
sth_masraf1,sth_masraf2,sth_masraf3,sth_masraf4,
sth_otvtutari,sth_oivtutari,sth_tip,
1,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_NET_DEGER_ALT,
dbo.fn_StokHareketNetDeger(sth_tutar,
sth_iskonto1,sth_iskonto2,sth_iskonto3,sth_iskonto4,sth_iskonto5,sth_iskonto6,
sth_masraf1,sth_masraf2,sth_masraf3,sth_masraf4,
sth_otvtutari,sth_oivtutari,sth_tip,
2,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_NET_DEGER_STOK_ORJ,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf1,0,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF1_ANA,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf1,1,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF1_ALT,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf1,2,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF1_STOK_ORJ,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf2,0,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF2_ANA,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf2,1,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF2_ALT,
dbo.fn_StokHareketBrutDeger(sth_masraf2,2,sth_har_doviz_kuru,sth_alt_doviz_kuru,sth_stok_doviz_kuru) AS STH_MASRAF2_STOK_ORJ
FROM dbo.STOK_HAREKETLERI SH WITH (NOLOCK , INDEX=NDX_STOK_HAREKETLERI_13)
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Stok_Hareket_Evrak_Isimleri SHEVRAK ON SHEvrNo=sth_evraktip
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Stok_Hareket_Cins_Isimleri  SHCINS  ON SHCinsNo=sth_cins
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Stok_Hareket_Tip_Isimleri   SHTIP   ON SHTipNo=sth_tip
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Normal_Iade_Isimleri        SHNI    ON NINo=sth_normal_iade
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.vw_Cari_Cins_Isimleri          SHCARICINS ON CCinsNo=sth_cari_cinsi
WHERE (sth_isemri_gider_kodu<>N'') AND(sth_cins IN (7,8))
GO
